 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#160;<span style="text-decoration:underline">2.02</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;14, 2021, Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the fiscal quarter and fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2021 and related matters. A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#160;<span style="text-decoration:underline">7.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Regulation FD Disclosure</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;14, 2021, the Company is conducting a Virtual Investor Day Conference beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time during which the Company will, among other items, discuss its results for the fiscal quarter and fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2021 and related matters. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Slides prepared for the purposes of the Virtual Investor Day Conference and slides related to the Company&#8217;s results for the fiscal quarter and fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2021 will be available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A link to the Virtual Investor Day Conference will be available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at: http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">9.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Financial Statements and Exhibits</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) <span style="text-decoration:underline">Exhibits</span> </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0%; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal Year 2021 Earnings </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">Fourth Quarter Results Exceed Expectations, Reflecting Strong Operational Performance and Surpassing Vaccination Goals </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Fourth quarter and fiscal year highlights </I></P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; adjusted EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1,2</SUP> increased 29.5&nbsp;percent to $1.17, up 28.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

11.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period; adjusted EPS increased 14.6&nbsp;percent to $4.91, up 13.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Net cash provided by operating activities in fiscal 2021 was $5.6&nbsp;billion, an increase of $70&nbsp;million compared
with fiscal 2020; Free cash flow was $4.2&nbsp;billion, up $65&nbsp;million year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Company delivered strong operational performance in
the fourth quarter </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><I></I>Results exceeded expectations across business segments </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Walgreens surpassed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccination goal, providing 13.5&nbsp;million
vaccinations in the quarter and 34.6&nbsp;million in fiscal 2021 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The company&#146;s Transformational Cost Management Program delivered in excess of $2&nbsp;billion in annual cost savings
by fiscal 2021, a year ahead of schedule </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Company leadership to discuss strategic priorities for the future and fiscal 2022 guidance at Virtual Investor Conference
today </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill., Oct. 14,&nbsp;2021 - Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the fiscal year
and fourth quarter that ended Aug. 31, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Chief Executive Officer Roz Brewer said, &#147;Our fourth quarter and fiscal year results exceeded expectations,
driven by strong performance in our core business. Comparable U.S. pharmacy and retail sales both saw robust growth and recovery continued in our UK business as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> restrictions eased in the quarter. I
remain extremely proud of our team members&#146; unwavering commitment to meeting the needs of our patients, customers and communities. The role of the pharmacist and local pharmacy is now more vital than ever.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Brewer added, &#147;I look forward to sharing more about the future of WBA at our Virtual Investor Conference today.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Fourth Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA fiscal 2021 fourth quarter sales
from continuing operations increased 12.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $34.3&nbsp;billion, up 11.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>,
reflecting strong growth in both the International and United States segments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income from continuing operations increased 49.7&nbsp;percent to
$910&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations increased 22.9&nbsp;percent on a reported currency basis to $1.2&nbsp;billion,
an increase of 22.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increase reflects strong gross profit growth across pharmacy and retail in the United States and higher International segment sales and profitability due to strong operational
performance and ongoing recovery in the UK, where <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> restrictions were lifted in July. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">1 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net earnings from continuing operations in the fourth quarter were $358&nbsp;million, up 6.4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting increased operating income in both segments. This was partially offset by higher tax provisions related to the enactment of the UK tax rate increase. Adjusted net earnings from
continuing operations increased 29.6&nbsp;percent to $1.0&nbsp;billion, up 28.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> from continuing operations increased 6.4&nbsp;percent to $0.41, compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations increased 29.5&nbsp;percent to $1.17, reflecting an increase of 28.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.2&nbsp;billion in the fourth quarter and free cash flow was $867&nbsp;million, an $808&nbsp;million decrease compared
with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter primarily due to the divestiture of the Alliance Healthcare business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Fiscal Year
Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Fiscal 2021 sales from continuing operations increased 8.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to
$132.5&nbsp;billion, up 7.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income from continuing
operations in fiscal 2021 increased to $2.3&nbsp;billion compared with $982&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. This was partly driven by $2&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT>
impairment charges in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. This was partially offset by a $1.5&nbsp;billion charge from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. Adjusted
operating income from continuing operations increased 8.2&nbsp;percent on a reported basis to $5.1&nbsp;billion, up 7.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increase reflects strong adjusted gross profit growth across the United States and
International segments, and cost savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net earnings from continuing operations were $2.0&nbsp;billion,
compared with $180&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, reflecting <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, strong
growth across both segments, and earnings from the company&#146;s equity method investment related to Option Care Health, partially offset by a charge from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. Adjusted net earnings from
continuing operations increased 12.8&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to $4.3&nbsp;billion, up 11.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> from continuing operations for fiscal 2021 increased to $2.30, compared with $0.20 in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $4.91, an increase of 14.6&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and an increase of 13.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $5.6&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2021, an increase of $70&nbsp;million from fiscal 2020, and free cash flow was
$4.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of $65&nbsp;million from fiscal 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">In line with the company&#146;s long-term capital policy to maintain a strong balance sheet
and financial flexibility, WBA reduced its leverage by approximately $6.5&nbsp;billion compared with the prior fiscal year end. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA continued to achieve strong results across its business, including: </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">WBA and VillageMD continued <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">roll-out</FONT> of Village Medical at Walgreens, with 52
primary care practice locations currently open, and will have more than 80 open by the end of calendar year 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Segments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>United States </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The United States segment had fourth quarter sales of
$28.8&nbsp;billion, an increase of 6.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable sales increased 8.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmacy sales increased 6.7&nbsp;percent and comparable pharmacy sales increased 8.9&nbsp;percent in the fourth quarter compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Within comparable pharmacy sales, prescriptions filled in the fourth quarter increased 8.8&nbsp;percent from a year earlier, including a positive impact of 485 basis points from <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter increased 8.6&nbsp;percent to 313&nbsp;million, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales increased 6.5&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales increased 6.2&nbsp;percent in the fourth quarter compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Excluding tobacco and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> they increased 7.2&nbsp;percent, reflecting broad based growth across all categories. In particular, health and
wellness sales increased 14&nbsp;percent aided by cough cold flu, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">at-home</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> tests and vitamins. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit increased 14.9&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted gross profit increased 13.7&nbsp;percent
due to strong sales growth; improved pharmacy margin, aided by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations partially offset by reimbursement; and favorable retail margin. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Selling, general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A) increased 12.9&nbsp;percent compared with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted
SG&amp;A increased 13.1&nbsp;percent driven by costs to support <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing, and from higher growth investments, partially offset by savings from the Transformational Cost Management
program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the fourth quarter increased 25.2&nbsp;percent to $1.0&nbsp;billion compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. Adjusted operating income increased 16.4&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion<I>.</I> </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">3 </FONT></P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The
International segment had fourth quarter sales of $5.5&nbsp;billion, an increase of 61.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 9.2&nbsp;percent. Sales increased
52.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, including higher sales associated with the formation of company&#146;s wholesale joint venture in Germany. Excluding this, International segment sales on a constant currency basis increased
9.3&nbsp;percent, reflecting the ongoing recovery in the UK market, where <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> restrictions were lifted on July 19. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased 11.4&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting stronger demand
for pharmacy services, notably <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> tests. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 15.0&nbsp;percent compared with
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Footfall on the high street recovered as lockdown measures were removed, although it remains below <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-COVID</FONT> levels. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots.com continued to perform ahead of expectations, with digital sales in the fourth quarter more than doubling compared with
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-COVID</FONT> levels. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit increased 43.0&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, including a favorable
currency impact of 10.4&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross profit increased 32.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting strong growth in retail sales and pharmacy services. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A in the quarter increased 19.0&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $1.2&nbsp;billion, including an adverse
currency impact of 8.2&nbsp;percent, offset by lower costs associated with the Transformational Cost Management Program in the current year. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased 17.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, including higher adjusted
SG&amp;A associated with the formation of the company&#146;s wholesale joint venture in Germany. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income, including a favorable currency impact of
6.1&nbsp;percent, was $46&nbsp;million compared with a loss of $130&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income grew strongly on a constant currency basis to $140&nbsp;million, an increase
of $129&nbsp;million compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Virtual Investor Conference </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA will hold a Virtual Investor Conference to discuss strategic priorities for the future, fiscal 2022 guidance and fourth quarter and fiscal 2021 earnings results
beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, Oct. 14, 2021. A live simulcast as well as related presentation materials will be available through WBA&#146;s investor relations website at: http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A replay of the
conference will be archived on the website for at least 12 months after the event. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is a
global leader in retail pharmacy, impacting millions of lives every day through dispensing medicines, and providing accessible, high-quality care. With more than 170 years of trusted healthcare heritage and innovation in community pharmacy, the
company is meeting customers&#146; and patients&#146; needs through its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA has a
presence in more than 9 countries, employs more than 315,000 people and has more than 13,000 stores in the U.S., Europe and Latin America. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA&#146;s purpose is to
inspire more joyful lives through better health. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA is a Participant of the United Nations Global Compact and
adheres to its principles-based approach to responsible business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">More company information is available at <FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(WBA-ER)</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><DIV ALIGN="right">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information
provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented
in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in
accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These
supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency
translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute
for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company does not provide
a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available
without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact
diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company also presents certain information related to
current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange
rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this
presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the company&#146;s United States and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least 12
consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months as well as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for
the first 12 months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable
retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. Comparable retail sales for previous periods have been restated to include <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. The method of calculating
comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which is
a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">9 </FONT></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company considers certain metrics, including all comparable metrics, number of prescriptions, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent
prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented
provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as
a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The Company recognized equity losses in AmerisourceBergen of
$1,373&nbsp;million during the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. These equity losses are primarily due to AmerisourceBergen&#146;s recognition of $5.6&nbsp;billion, net of tax, charges related to its ongoing opioid litigation in its
financial statements for the three months period ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and inventory valuation
adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangibles assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired or the estimated useful life of an intangible
asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to measure acquired inventory at fair value. The fair value of the inventory reflects
cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments exclude the expected profit margin component from cost of sales recorded under the business combination accounting
principles. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program and Store Optimization Program charges are costs associated with a formal
restructuring plan. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain legal
proceedings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating
performance. These charges are recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include all charges incurred on certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities, for example, including costs related to integration efforts for successful merger, acquisition and
divestitures activities. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related
activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Goodwill and intangible assets arising from acquisition related activities are recorded by the Company following the
analysis to determine the fair value of consideration paid and the assignment of fair values to all tangible and intangible assets acquired. Impairment of goodwill and intangible assets do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s
business. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating
performance. These charges are recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s United States segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the United States segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be
impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Store damage and inventory losses as a result of looting in the U.S., net of insurance recoveries. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in foreign
subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within other income (expense). We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying
derivative instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

Company recorded a gain of $290&nbsp;million in Other income due to a partial sale of ownership interests in Option Care Health by the Company&#146;s equity method investee HC Group Holdings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

$3.3&nbsp;billion of long term U.S. denominated notes. The Company excludes these charges to enable a more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s financial performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax provision commensurate with <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income tax provision (benefit).
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax equity earnings from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share of certain
equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded within
post tax earnings (loss) from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity
method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that
they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. In the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021 due to partial sales of ownership interests in Option Care Health, our equity method investee HC Group Holdings lost the
ability to control Option Care Health and, therefore, deconsolidated Option Care Health in its financial statements. As a result of this deconsolidation, HC Group Holdings recognized a gain of $1.2&nbsp;billion and the Company recorded its share of
equity earnings in HC Group Holdings of $576&nbsp;million during the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

month reporting lag, operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2021 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings (loss) for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2021 through June&nbsp;30, 2021 and the period of
July&nbsp;1, 2020 through June&nbsp;30, 2021, respectively. Operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2020 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2020 through

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Operating income (loss) for United States includes equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen. As a result of the two
month reporting lag, operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2021 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings (loss) for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2021 through June&nbsp;30, 2021 and the period of
July&nbsp;1, 2020 through June&nbsp;30, 2021, respectively. Operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2020 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2020 through
June&nbsp;30, 2020, and the period of July&nbsp;1, 2019 through June&nbsp;30, 2020, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Operating margins and adjusted operating margins have been calculated excluding equity earnings (loss) in
AmerisourceBergen and adjusted equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">17 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual
obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;# </P>

</DIV></Center>
